# Oshio Heihachiro
japanese_flavor_Oshio_Heihachiro = {
	first_name = japanese_flavor_Oshio_Heihachiro_first
	last_name = japanese_flavor_Oshio_Heihachiro_last
	culture = cu:japanese
	female = no
	ideology = ideology_abolitionist
	interest_group = ig_devout
	birth_date = 1793.1.1
	trait_generation = { set_variable = historical_figure }
	traits = {
		concept_wikipedia_Oshio_Heihachiro
		charismatic
		inspirational_orator
		firebrand
	}
	interest_group_leader_usage = {
		country_trigger = {
			exists = c:JAP
			this = c:JAP
		}
		interest_group_trigger = {
			is_interest_group_type = ig_devout
		}
		earliest_usage_date = 1823.1.1
		latest_usage_date = 1837.12.31
		chance = 75
	}
}
